 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">The information in this Current Report on Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;8-K</span> is being furnished and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities under that Section and shall not be deemed to be incorporated by reference into any filing of the Registrant under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, unless specifically identified therein as being incorporated by reference. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;7.01. </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Regulation&#160;FD Disclosure.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. (&#8220;Mondel&#275;z International,&#8221; the &#8220;Company,&#8221; &#8220;we,&#8221; &#8220;us&#8221; and &#8220;our&#8221; ) is providing the disclosure below and supplementing the risk factors described in Item&#160;1A of the Company&#8217;s Annual Report on Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;10-K</span> for the year ended December&#160;31, 2019 (the &#8220;Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;10-K&#8221;)</span> with the following risk factor, which the Company included in a preliminary prospectus supplement, dated April&#160;7, 2020, in connection with an offering of debt securities (the &#8220;Preliminary Prospectus&#8221;). The information in this report on Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;8-K</span> should be read in conjunction with the risk factors described in the Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;10-K</span> and the information under the &#8220;Forward-Looking Statements&#8221; in the Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;10-K. </span></p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">The following supplemental disclosure was included in the Preliminary Prospectus </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Recent Developments </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Impact of <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19 </span></p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">The rapid, worldwide spread of <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> has created global economic disruption and uncertainty, including in our business. As a result, we expect higher sales in some markets and channels, such as the United States and some European markets and modern trade (including large grocery supermarkets and retail chains) during this period, as consumers significantly increase their current food purchases for <span style="white-space:nowrap">in-home</span> consumption, especially for some categories like biscuits. We also expect lower revenues during this period in some of our emerging market countries that have a higher concentration of traditional trade outlets (such as small <span style="white-space:nowrap">family-run</span> stores), as well as in our travel retail (such as international duty-free stores) and foodservice businesses, all of which are negatively impacted by enforced lockdowns. See &#8220;Risk Factors&#8212;Global or regional health pandemics or epidemics, including <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</span> could negatively impact our business operations, financial performance and results of operations.&#8221; </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:Bold;font-style:Italic;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Revolving Credit Agreements </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On March&#160;6, 2020, we entered into a revolving credit agreement (the &#8220;$2.5 Billion Revolving Credit Agreement&#8221;) for a <span style="white-space:nowrap">364-day </span>&#32;senior unsecured revolving credit facility in an aggregate principal amount of $2.5&#160;billion with the lenders named in the $2.5&#160;Billion Revolving Credit Agreement, and JPMorgan Chase Bank, N.A. as administrative agent. On March&#160;12, 2020, we borrowed $1.0&#160;billion principal amount under the $2.5&#160;Billion Revolving Credit Agreement as a strategic decision to have cash on hand in light of current uncertainty in the global markets resulting from the <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> outbreak. On April&#160;1, 2020, we borrowed an additional $1.25&#160;billion principal amount under the $2.5&#160;Billion Revolving Credit Agreement to fund the completion of our previously announced acquisition of Give&#160;&#038; Go Prepared Foods Corp. As of April&#160;6, 2020, we have borrowed $2.25&#160;billion principal amount under the $2.5&#160;Billion Revolving Credit Agreement. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">On March&#160;24, 2020, we entered into a revolving credit agreement (as amended, the &#8220;$1.95&#160;Billion Revolving Credit Agreement&#8221;) for a <span style="white-space:nowrap">364-day</span> senior unsecured revolving credit facility in an aggregate principal amount of $1.75&#160;billion with the lenders named in the $1.95&#160;Billion Revolving Credit Agreement; and Citibank, N.A. as administrative agent. On April&#160;1, 2020, we entered into a first amendment commitment increase of $200&#160;million with the administrative agent and BNP Paribas, increasing to $1.95&#160;billion aggregate principal amount available under the $1.95&#160;Billion Revolving Credit Agreement. As of April&#160;6, 2020, we had no borrowings under the $1.95&#160;Billion Revolving Credit Agreement. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-style:italic;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">The following risk factor was included in the Preliminary Prospectus </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt">Global or regional health pandemics or epidemics, including <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</span> could negatively impact our business operations, financial performance and results of operations. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">Our business and financial results could be negatively impacted by the recent outbreak of <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> or other pandemics or epidemics. The severity, magnitude and duration of the current <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> pandemic is uncertain, rapidly changing and hard to predict. In 2020, <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> has significantly impacted economic activity and markets around the world, and it could negatively impact our business in numerous ways, including but not limited to those outlined below: </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">We expect the <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> outbreak to result in lower revenues in some of our emerging market countries that have a higher concentration of traditional trade outlets (such as small <span style="white-space:nowrap">family-run</span> stores), as well as in our travel retail (such as international duty-free stores) and foodservice businesses.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">In addition, we expect increased sales of some of our products for <span style="white-space:nowrap">in-home</span> consumption that are currently in demand in some markets and channels, such as the United States and some European markets and modern trade. We are unable to predict how long this sustained demand will last or how significant it will be.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Commodity costs have become more volatile due to the <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> outbreak. We expect continued commodity cost volatility, and our commodity hedging activities might not sufficiently offset this volatility.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">The <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> outbreak could disrupt our global supply chain, operations and routes to market or those of our suppliers, their suppliers, or our <span style="white-space:nowrap">co-manufacturers</span> or distributors. These disruptions or our failure to effectively respond to them could increase product or distribution costs or cause delays in delivering or an inability to deliver products to our customers. We have experienced temporary disruptions in certain emerging markets operations such as India and Nigeria that to date have not been material to our consolidated results.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Disruptions or uncertainties related to the <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> outbreak for a sustained period of time could result in delays or modifications to our strategic plans and initiatives and hinder our ability to achieve our objective to reduce our operating cost structure in both our supply chain and overhead costs through our Simplify to Grow Program.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Illness, travel restrictions or workforce disruptions could negatively affect our supply chain, manufacturing, distribution or other business processes.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Government or regulatory responses to pandemics could negatively impact our business. Mandatory lockdowns or other restrictions on operations in some countries have temporarily disrupted our ability to distribute our products in some of these markets. Continuation or expansion of these disruptions could materially adversely impact our operations and results.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">We expect to be negatively impacted by currency translation losses from a generally stronger U.S. dollar relative to other currencies in the countries in which we operate. These along with currency transaction losses could adversely affect our reported results of operations and financial condition.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
<tr style="page-break-inside:avoid;">
<td style="width:5%;text-align:left;">&#160;</td>
<td style="width:3%;vertical-align:top;">&#8226;</td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">The <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> outbreak has increased volatility and pricing in the capital markets and commercial paper markets, and volatility is likely to continue. We might not be able to continue to access preferred sources of liquidity when we would like, and our borrowing costs could increase.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">These and other impacts of the <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> or other global or regional health pandemics or epidemics could have the effect of heightening many of the other risks described in this &#8220;Risk Factors&#8221; section and those incorporated by reference herein, such as those relating to our reputation, brands, product sales, </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
 </div>



<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%" />

 <div style="font-size:10pt;width:8.5in;margin:0 auto"> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt">results of operations or financial condition. We might not be able to predict or respond to all impacts on a timely basis to prevent near- or long-term adverse impacts to our results. The ultimate impact of these disruptions also depends on events beyond our knowledge or control, including the duration and severity of any outbreak and actions taken by parties other than us to respond to them. Any of these disruptions could have a negative impact on our business operations, financial performance and results of operations, which impact could be material. </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:24pt">FORWARD-LOOKING STATEMENTS </p> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;text-indent:4%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:12pt">This Current Report on Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;8-K</span> contains a number of forward-looking statements. Words, and variations of words, such as &#8220;will,&#8221; &#8220;expect,&#8221; &#8220;would,&#8221; &#8220;could,&#8221; &#8220;might,&#8221; &#8220;plan,&#8221; &#8220;likely,&#8221; and similar expressions are intended to identify our forward-looking statements, including but not limited to statements about the impact of the recent outbreak of the novel coronavirus <span style="white-space:nowrap">(&#8220;COVID-19&#8221;) </span>&#32;pandemic. These forward-looking statements involve risks and uncertainties, many of which are beyond our control, and many of these risks and uncertainties are currently amplified by and may continue to be amplified by, or in the future may be amplified by, the <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> outbreak. Important factors that could cause actual results to differ materially from those described in our forward-looking statements include, but are not limited to, uncertainty of the magnitude, duration, geographic reach, impact on the global economy and current and potential travel restrictions of the <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</span> outbreak; the current, and uncertain future, impact of the <span style="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19 </span>&#32;outbreak on our business, growth, reputation, prospects, financial condition, operating results (including components of our financial results), cash flows and liquidity; and the other risks and uncertainties described in the &#8220;Risk Factors&#8221; section under Item&#160;1A of Part&#160;I of our Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;10-K</span> and &#8220;Forward-Looking Statements&#8221; under Item 1 of Part I of our Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;10-K,</span> as such discussions may be further updated by subsequent filings we make with the Securities and Exchange Commission. We disclaim and do not undertake any obligation to update or revise any forward-looking statement in this Current Report on Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;8-K</span> except as required by applicable law or regulation. </p> <div></div> <p style="margin-top:1em;margin-bottom:0em"></p>
